评论人：[夏季的橙子]
评论时间：2017-12-27
评论标题：有哪些以小兔子为主角的可爱的故事？
评论内容：答主作为软萌兔子的狂热爱好者，在英国的水石书店里发现了好多可爱的兔子故事。慢慢更。1.《Guess how much I love YOU》猜猜我有多爱你主角是一对兔子父子~这对小兔子因为太受欢迎有很多可爱的周边，这是答主收藏的一版小兔子讲自己对大兔子的爱有张开手臂那么长，大兔子也张开了手臂，更长更长。我爱你，像我能跳到的距离！我爱你的距离，超越草地和河流。我爱你，像飞向月亮又回来的距离。再放几张可爱的图2. 《The Tale of Peter Rabbit》彼得潘小兔的故事这只小兔子感觉很像英国的国兔了，绘本由Beatrix Potter创造。主角是一只身穿天蓝色毛线衫的棕色小兔子。她有温柔的妈妈，调皮的兄弟姐妹，还有其他很多有趣的小伙伴。Beatrix的灵感来源于英国湖区美丽的自然风光和乡下各种可爱的小动物。彼得兔一家。陶醉地偷吃胡萝卜。被农夫发现啦！！快跑。妈妈给小兔子系扣子。和小鸟们玩耍。其实我特别喜欢这个很像哲学家的青蛙先生啦。3.《Vetreteen the Rabbit， how toys become real》玩具小兔变形记这是一个很温暖的故事，一只毛绒玩具小兔子陪伴小男孩度过了整个同年。在她失去光泽破败不堪的时候，因为曾经得到了孩子最真挚的爱，它变成了一只真正的小兔子！未完待续。

评论人：[Elon Liu]
评论时间：2017-12-23
评论标题：有什么非常经典的说唱歌词吗？
评论内容：分不同类先列几个，有空再加。1. Freestyle / Rap Battles说到 freestyle 或者 battles, 肯定要提一代传奇欧阳靖（MC Jin）啊，在美国 106 &amp; Park 节目里蝉联7周冠军，连挫黑人，荡气回肠，够不够经典？My pants are new, my sweater is new. Don\'t be mad at Chinese kid dressed better than you.—— Jin (vs. Sean Nicholas)You wanna say I\'m Chinese sonny? Here\'s a remindaCheck your Timbs they probably say "made in China"—— Jin (vs. Sterling)2. 影视作品中的 Rap BattlesEminem 的自传电影 8 Miles，因为讲的就是自己经历过的生活，所以有很多 rap battle 的演绎，也颇为经典。Don\'t ever try to judge me, dudeYou don\'t know what the fuck I\'ve been through—— Eminem as B-Rabbit (vs. Papa Doc)This guy don\'t wanna battle, he shook\'Cause ain\'t no such things as halfway crooks—— Eminem as B-Rabbit (vs. Papa Doc)这一句是灵活化用了 Mobb Deep 的歌 Shook Ones 里的词，引起所有听众群声附和，气势拔群。另外一个节目是后来发现的柯登深夜秀里有个 Drop the Mic 的表演，是嘉宾明星跟柯登对飙，估计词是准备好的，制造效果。不过挺有意思的。女神 Anne Hathaway 也来过！I was hated and shaded but now I been liberatedThere\'s nothing you can say to leave me incapacitated—— Anne Hathaway (in Drop the Mic)还有一个强烈安利的视频叫 Epic Rap Battles of History，是油管上两个家伙做的说唱视频，每一期扮演两个历史人物进行对战，表演和用词都挺有意思的。列举几例：I need to bring up some basic shitWhy\'d you name your company after your dick?—— Nice Peter as Steve Jobs (in Epic Rap Battles of History)乔布斯嘲笑比尔盖茨“又微又软”……I\'m as dope as two rappers, you better be scaredCuz that means Albert E. equals MC squared—— MC Mr Napkins as Albert Einstein (in Epic Rap Battles of History)爱因斯坦的 E=mc2，MC 双关了（这也行……）I\'m the giant whose shoulders you\'d have stood on if you could standI\'ll give you a brief history of pain with the back of my hand—— MC Mr Napkins as Albert Einstein (in Epic Rap Battles of History)爱因斯坦怼霍金，我就是你所站在的巨人肩膀的那个巨人，哦，你站不起来…… 也是够贱了…… 霍金的《时间简史》也被调戏成耳光简史了。绝了。3. 专辑歌曲作品这里面就比较多了。先上 Jay-Z 的 99 Problems：If you\'re havin\' girl problems, I feel bad for you, sonI got 99 problems, but a bitch ain\'t one—— Jay-Z 99 Problems这一句被广大 Rappers 化用极多啊，比如 Eminem 的：I got 99 problems and a bitch ain\'t oneShe\'s all 99 of \'em, I need a machine gun—— Eminem So Much Better提到 Eminem，那经典歌词就多了去了。See, honey, there\'s a place called Heaven and a place called HellA place called prison and a place called jailAnd Dada\'s probably on his way to all of \'em except one\'Cause Mama\'s got a new husband and a stepson—— Eminem 97\' Bonnie &amp; Clyde万劫不复，只因老婆离自己而去……They make it all up, there\'s no such thingLike a female with good looks who cooks and cleans—— Eminem Business老婆点评说这句不对，她自己就是反例……I guess words are a motherfucker, they can be greatOr they can degrade, or even worse, they can teach hate—— Eminem Sing for the MomentDaddy\'s gonna buy you a mockingbirdI\'ma give you the worldI\'ma buy a diamond ring for you, I\'ma sing for youI\'ll do anything for you to see you smileAnd if that mockingbird don\'t sing and that ring don\'t shineI\'ma break that birdie\'s neckI\'ll go back to the jeweler who sold it to yaAnd make him eat every carat, don\'t fuck with Dad!—— Eminem MockingbirdMockingbird 本来是个哄小孩的歌曲 (nursing song)，被 Eminem 整得如此暴力也是没谁了。就是这种近似变态的表述，却把对自己女儿不顾一切的爱表达得特别动人。I could\'ve either just sat on my assAnd pissed and moanedOr take this situation in which I\'m placed inAnd get up and get my own—— Eminem BeautifulWhy do we say that until we get that person that we think\'sGonna be that one, then once we get \'em it\'s never the sameYou want them when they don\'t want youSoon as they do, feelings change—— Eminem Space Bound多到列举不过来，以霸气的一句暂时结束：Don\'t be a retard – be a king? Think notWhy be a king when you can be a god?—— Eminem Rap God
